< Text>
Love their breakfast plate, which comes with scramble eggs (you should ask for Salvadoran style which comes with veggies) refried beans, fried plantains and hand made tortillas, and you can get it at any time day or night. I also like their fried corn tamale. Their pupusas are ok and I usually order cheese with zucchini. I come here from time to time cause they close until 11pm which is rear for a Salvadoran restaurant to close that late. The place is at times way too loud cause their music takes over the whole place and to have a conversation you need to be louder than usual. Also the place is not as dirty but their bathroom I will use only for emergencies. The area is parking meter only, but since I usually go in the night is free.< /Text>

We made reservations for a big group.  They were helpful and patient.  It was a mellow vibe.  We came during happy hour and the beers were massive. We ordered meatballs, deep fried cauliflower, sliders, sandwiches, pizzas etc.

It turned into karaoke at 9pm on a Thursday.  Then it got crowded.  Too crowded.  A lot of baseball hats.  Bro city.</Review>

< Review>
I went to Tower 12 today to meet a friend from the East Coast who was visiting in town. We wanted to pick a place that was low-key and casual but had good food and a good atmosphere. We were not disappointed. The proprietor was the nicest gentleman and made me feel right at home the minute I sat down at the bar while I waited for my friend to join me. We had a long discussion about music and about the local beach scene. Our food was very good we had the Hawaiian style pizza meatball sliders and truffle fries. I'm one of the best things was just the location itself period on a hot summer day it was nice to have a little breeze flowing through an open-air space where we could keep cool and still feel like we are outside enjoying the beach. <Review>The Hermosa Beach Pier promenade is a happening place to visit. The location of the Tower 12 restaurant has been around for a long time but under another name.  It has been a local hangout where locals go during the week. Tourist flock there on weekends to hang out upstairs at one of their 2 bars and scope out the bikini babes below on Pier's walking promenade. If your in to  beers and  burgers  type places them this is your place. It can get pretty loud on holidays and weekends. But then most of the restaurants on Pier do also. If your looking for a quiet romantic place looking for that California sunset, this is not for you. Swimsuit and flip-flops are the norm. Their single cheese burger has 2 beef patties and the double cheese burger has 3 they say because the patties are thin. They do however have a good happy hour with 32oz tap beers and 22oz mixed drinks.

A Local Patron</Review>< Pictures>

My group of friends watched this all go down... they wouldn't let a group of black and asian folks go in but they sure let white folks go in. I was super disappointed to say the least as I love going to Hermosa Beach and frequent there often. I have never come across this type of behavior at other establishments on the pier.
